//server/routes/routes.js
var express = require('express');
var router = express.Router();
var bodyParser = require('body-parser');
var mongoose = require('mongoose');

//multer
//CXg[
const multer = require('multer')

// Google Cloud Vision
//
// uncommentgoogleANZXG[NAAA
// const vision = require('@google-cloud/vision');
// const client = new vision.ImageAnnotatorClient();

const storage = multer.diskStorage({

//multerfilesavew
destination : function(req, file, cb){
cb(null, './uploads/')
},

//filefilename w
filename : function(req, file, cb){
// cb(null, new Date().toISOString() + file.originalname);
cb(null, file.originalname);
},
})

//uploadt@Cw
const fileFilter = (req, file, cb) => {
// only accept .jpen and .png file type 
if (file.mimetype === 'image/jpeg' || file.mimetype === 'image/png') {
cb(null, true);
} else {
cb(null, false);
}
};

const upload = multer({
storage : storage,
limits: {
fileSize: 1024 * 1024 * 5
},
fileFilter : fileFilter
});

router.get('/', function(req, res){
res.render('index')
});

// GET METHOD
router.get("/uploadImage", (req, res, next) => {

const imageModel = require('../../models/imageModel');
imageModel.find()
.select("name price _id image")
.exec()
.then(docs => {
const response = {
count: docs.length,
products: docs.map(doc => {
return {
name: doc.name,
price: doc.price,
image: doc.image,
_id: doc._id,
request: {
type: "GET",
url: "http://localhost:8000/imageModel/" + doc._id
}
};
})
};
// if (docs.length >= 0) {
res.status(200).json(response);
// } else {
// res.status(404).json({
// message: 'No entries found'
// });
// }
})
.catch(err => {
console.log(err);
res.status(500).json({
error: err
});
});
});

// POST METHOD
router.post('/uploadImage', upload.single("image"), (req, res, next) => {
/*
how to test in post man

url : http://localhost:8000/uploadImage
in body > form-data >
create: price (text), name(text), image(file) 
https://qiita.com/sn6t/items/a18fd511035d6d9385de
*/
console.log(req.file)
const imageModel = require('../../models/imageModel');
const newImage = new imageModel({
_id : new mongoose.Types.ObjectId(),
name : req.body.name,
price : req.body.price,
image : req.file.path 
});

newImage
.save()
.then(result => {
console.log(result)
res.status(201).json({
message : "created product successfully",
createdProduct: {
name : result.name,
price: result.price,
_id : result._id,
request: {
type: 'GET',
url: "http://localhost:8000/uploadImage/" + result._id
}
}
})
})
});

module.exports = router;
